msg:Ctrip shows that this is a 5-star hotel? I think it is 3 stars at most! Why?
First, the gate staff chatted and did not provide service. There were 4 of us with big and small bags, holding a child and dragging a little friend. There were two people at the lobby door, but when they saw that we had a lot of things, they did not take the initiative to help, but chatted? This is not the service of a 5-star hotel!
Second, the check-in, the front desk business is not proficient. There are obviously 4 check-in counters, and there are 4 staff on site, but they opened two for us to queue? Two were busy and two were chatting in the back. After waiting for a few minutes, I found that there were too many people and opened an extra position for processing. The process was unskilled and slow!
Third, there are a lot of priced consumer items in the room. The room price is 600 and they are still using the routine of ordinary hotels. Although they say that they don‚Äôt have to pay if they don‚Äôt open it, this makes people feel a little disgusting, which is not what a 5-star hotel should show!
Fourth, the room type is randomly arranged and they want to deceive. I booked 4 cloud rooms on the platform of Ctrip 4 days in advance, 3 large beds and 1 double bed. It should be a family trip, so I noted that I hope to be on the same floor. After placing the order, the hotel also called to confirm and promised to arrange it for me.
As a result, they did arrange the same floor, but the twin room was reduced in size. Compared with the above picture, there was no bathtub! The area was small! Obviously not a cloud room. I called them to ask for analysis and processing. On the first call, they replied that they could only arrange this room because the room was full today (implying that it was not available if I stayed or not?). I was a little annoyed and argued with them, and then they told me to wait for a call back. On the second call, more than ten minutes later, they couldn't help but call them again, and they replied that there was no room on the same floor and they couldn't change it! Are you asking for a scolding? You promised to arrange the room I booked early in the morning, but now you messed it up and didn't even say sorry, and you still handled it with this attitude?
I said: I insisted on booking a cloud room! You have to arrange what I booked for me, and you can't reduce it!
The third call came, telling me that there are cloud twin rooms on other floors! Even more angry, you said so much before that there was no room today and couldn't change it. Is this monkey hair? I have never seen such a shameless 5-star hotel. The room type was reduced and it was blamed on the full room. If there was a room to change, I felt that the service was heavenly! How did you want to fool the guests after being discovered!
Summary: No value for money, high price and poor service! The location is remote, there is nothing to eat nearby, and there is no river view. I define this as an apartment hotel, not a 5-star hotel.
